 Pradhan Kai was all told in UP Bharai, not understood, he was blinded by his eyes, Lakhon Morga was sacrificed, not Daru Luhan on contract, all farming was sold, Lutan Dihin Tabou won not Pradhan
 '' yah us kavita kii chand line hai jise karnalganj main rahane vaale kisaan kripashankar mishra ne pradhan par vyangïya karte hue likhaa he
 Amarendra Tripathi, a video of Kripa Shankar saying this poem while standing in the field, shared the Facebook page 'awadhi Bhasha' in his Khalis Awadhi in August last year
 iske baad to is kavita ne tahalaka machaa diya
 So far, more than 25 lakh people have heard this poem and more than 50,000 people have shared it
 desh main avadhi kii pehali website 'avadhi bhashaa' main amrendra treepathi ab tak kisaan kripashankar jaise saikadon aise logon kii avadhi rachanaaon ko post kar chuke hai jinhen kavi kaa darja to nahin mila lekin unki kavitaayen chautarafa dhooma machaa rahi hai
 This is the reason that in 2010, 'awadhi Bhasha', the Facebook page dedicated to Awadhi, not only has more than 22,000 followers, but this page has received more than 2
5 million likes
 avadhi bhashaa ke jariye logon ko ek manch par jodgaye kaa prayaas kar rahe amrendra treepathi patna ke patliputra vishvavidhyalay main assistant professor hai
 Amarendra's father Rajendra Nath Tripathi, a resident of Purva village of Lonakhar in Milkipur, Tehsil of Uttar Pradesh's Ayodhya district, was a teacher of sociology
 snaatak tak kii padhai amrendra ne gaanv main hi rahakar kii
 Amarendra had a connection with Awadhi language since childhood
 aise main yah inke astitv se jud gai thi
 In the year 2003, Amarendra enrolled in MA Hindi at Jawaharlal Nehru University (JNU), Delhi
 amrendra bataate hai, ''jeenyu main avadhi ko lekar kaaphi virodhabhasi mahaul tha
 It was not accepted as a language
 '' jeenyu main pard rahe avadh ilaake se aae logon se avadhi ko alag pahchaan dilaane ke liye koi kaarykram shuru karne kaa prayaas kiya lekin safal na ho sake
 After doing MA and mphil in Hindi literature, in 2009 while doing phd in Hindi literature at JNU, Amarendra started posting the poems of the poets of Awadhi by creating the blog of 'awadhi Kai Arghan' i
e
 Avadhi's fragrance
 ramai kaaka, balbhadra prasad dikshit padhis, adyaprasad singh unmakt, jumay khan aaazaad, bekal utsaahi, parasnath mishra bhramar jaise kaviyon kii rachanaaen 'avadhi kai arghan' blog main pramukhataa se post hone lageen
 Amarendra says, "since the compositions of these Awadhi poets were popular among the people, the blog became increasingly popular as their compilation was found in one place
 ''avadhi ke is blog kii lokapriyata badaae ke baad 2010 main amrendra ne 'avadhi kai arghan' ke naam se desh kii pehali avadhi website launch kii jiskaa yuarel 'avadh
 Org 'was
 is website main avadhi ke namchin kaviyon ke alaava un saamaanya logon kii rachanaaen bhi prakashit honi shuru huin jo shaukia taur par kavita likhte the

 There is good news for lawyers in Madhya Pradesh amid the intense heat wave
 vakeelon ko 15 april se agle teen maheene tak pairvi ke vakt kaala kot pahanane se chhot mil gai he
 Sources in the State Advocates Council today said that the council's executive committee took the decision in view of the problems faced by lawyers wearing black coats during the summer season
 yah faisla baar council of india ke sambandhit niyam ke mutabik kiya gaya
 This decision will be effective from April 15 to July 15 in the state
 sutron ke mutabik kaala kot pahanane kii chhot ke daayre main aane vaale purush vakeelon ko pairvi ke vakt pehle kii tarah safed shart, kaala yaa safed yaa grey rang kaa dharidaar pant pahananaa hoga
 Also, a special white bandage (advocate band) will be placed around the neck
 sutron ne haalanki spasht kiya ki vakeelon ke kaala kot pahanane kii chhot supreme court or hoicourt main pairvi ke vakt lagu nahin hogi
 Meanwhile, Gopal Kacholia, former secretary of the Indore District Bar Association, said that the attorneys get sweaty when they wear black coats during the scorching heat, which causes them a lot of trouble while appearing in court
 kacholia ke mutabik pradesh ke adhikansh jila or tehsil adhivaktaa sanghon ke karyaalayon main vakeelon ke baithne kii jagah unki badi taadaad ke mukaable behad kam he
 As a result, most of the lawyers often sit in the verandah of the court building and the open space outside it to handle their urgent work
